Public Security Bureau Issues Another Notice Yesterday

Deadline for Smokers to Renew Licenses Approaching

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau has been handling the renewal of the second phase of licenses, following the deadline, which will end at the end of this month. According to the assessment, 80% of the smokers who have renewed their licenses have complied with the regulations in the first phase of registration. There are still a few smokers who have not complied with the regulations to renew their licenses. The bureau recently issued another notice yesterday, as the deadline is only ten days away, in order to urge smokers who have not renewed their licenses to renew their licenses as soon as possible, so that smokers pay attention. The original text of the notice is recorded as follows: The investigation of the renewal of the second phase of smoking cessation licenses will expire on June 30. There are only ten days left before the end of the renewal. If you still do not renew the license after the deadline, the old license will be invalid. Once discovered, you will be severely punished. The bureau is sincerely afraid that a few smokers do not understand the strict prohibition order, so it is hereby notified for your information. You must go to the responsible branch office where you live to register and renew your license before June 30, and do not delay any longer to avoid violating the law. Special notice.

The bureau dispatched a large number of investigators and long-term police officers to investigate smokers as the deadline for license renewal approached, and the work was very tense. Yesterday, more than 70 unlicensed smokers were found and are being interrogated separately, it is said.

Jiangsu Provincial Government and Shanghai Banking Circles Organize Northern Jiangsu Salt Reclamation Banking Syndicate

Minimum Amount of 6 Million Yuan Being Negotiated. 2 Million People Can Have Food After Reclamation

According to the Huadong News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Cotton Industry Compilation Committee invited Shanghai banking circles on the 10th of this month to form a inspection group for the inspection of salt reclamation in northern Jiangsu, which has now returned to Shanghai. It is learned that the Jiangsu Provincial Government is eager to develop this wasteland and has invited banks in Shanghai to organize a salt reclamation banking syndicate. It is reported that the minimum amount is 6 million yuan, which is being negotiated. However, the success period is still far away. If it can be reclaimed as arable land, 2 million people can hope to have food to eat. More than 1 million Jiangsu natives in Shanghai can return to their hometowns and live and work in peace. The details are as follows:

Jiangsu Province Asks to Form a Salt Reclamation Banking Syndicate After inviting banking circles to visit northern Jiangsu, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has been making great efforts to develop the barren land that can be planted with cotton. During the inspection, they repeatedly discussed with representatives of various banks. The province intends that the minimum amount should be 6 million yuan to facilitate development. However, the banking circles believe that this is not comparable to a simple short-term investment for business purposes. Although they have agreed, they have not made a concrete statement.

The Salt Reclamation Area Is Very Peaceful According to a financial expert who returned to Shanghai with the group yesterday, the results of this trip yielded a lot of information. Politically, it has made a lot of progress compared to when Zhang Gongquan, then general manager of the Bank of China, and others went to northern Jiangsu in the seventh year of the Republic of China. Bandits have disappeared and the local area is peaceful. Technically, there has been no progress in the past ten years. People mostly use old methods for planting. The total area of salt land in northern Jiangsu is more than 15 million mu, of which only more than 2 million mu have been reclaimed. All the sovereignty belongs to the reclamation company, so farmers have no sense of security and are unwilling to cultivate the fields diligently. This is because it is a tenant farmer nature, and has nothing to do with them after the reclamation. The capital of the salt reclamation companies is too small, and they are only focused on commercial competition and have no permanent plan. The provincial government is also involved in preventing this, which may make it difficult to attract investment from the financial community. The people are hard-working and the local area is peaceful. If the management is improved in the future, it is very promising.

Improved Management, Unlimited Future The existing 2 million mu of reclaimed salt land yields about 5 yuan per mu each year, with a total annual income of 10 million yuan, which can support more than 300,000 people. If all the management is mature in the future, the future will be unlimited. 15 million mu of cotton land can allow more than 500,000 households to make a living. Counting four people in a family, 2 million people can make a living from this. Each mu of land yields at least 5 yuan per year (more is unlimited), with a total annual income of more than 75 million yuan to more than 100 million yuan. The civilians in Shanghai who are waiting for food can all develop to the salt reclamation area, which is less than a thousand miles away. At the same time, the annual production of 10,000 yuan of cotton can also prevent the import of foreign cotton of the same value (this cotton can be spun into 16 to 20 count coarse yarn), which is beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood. It all depends on the cooperation of the government, the financial community, and the people.

Pan Yangyao Talks About the Prerequisites According to the New New News Agency, the Shanghai Banking Circle and the Cotton Industry Compilation Committee's inspection group for the northern Jiangsu salt reclamation area returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday. A reporter from the New New News Agency interviewed Mr. Pan Yangyao, the director of the investigation section of the Four Banks Savings Association, who participated in the group. According to him, all the salt reclamation areas in the trip have been passed through. It is estimated that the barren land that needs to be reclaimed is about 15 million mu, and only one-fifth of it has been reclaimed. Therefore, most of it is unreclaimed wasteland. According to the observations, there are three major shortcomings. Firstly, the past reclamation companies competed too much for profits. Secondly, there was no political assistance. Fifthly, there was a lack of excellent technology. Therefore, there has been no special progress in the past few years. Therefore, the banking circles know that this place is a good area for investing in rural areas, after the opening of the new canal from Nantong Jiaoxie to Chenjiagang in Haizhou, the development of rural areas has increased hope. However, for the sake of stable investment, the following problems must be solved before investment. First, political assistance, because various places in northern Jiangsu are extremely barren, bandits are rampant, and security needs to be handled by the government. Second, traffic is blocked. The reclaimed area is vast, and the transportation of agricultural products by land and water is very inconvenient. Third, soil research. The soil geology in the reclaimed area is uneven, and it must be tested first to know what should be planted where. Fourth, water conservancy research. The ports and rivers in the reclaimed area are mostly silted, and attention must also be paid to facilitate irrigation. As for the hard work and thrift of farmers in various places, they are indeed the crown of various counties in Jiangsu Province, but the hardship of life is also greater than that of various counties in Jiangnan. The rewards they have worked so hard for all year round are not enough to keep them warm and fed. The main reason is that they are exploited by commercial loans. Most of the farmers in the reclaimed area are residents of Qidong and Haimen, but they are not good at saving. The price of their hard work is mostly spent on smoking, drinking, and gambling. They do not care about the suffering of ordinary times when they have money. This is also greatly related to civilian education, it is said.

Ministry of Communications: Outline of Measures for Reorganizing the Shipping Industry - Opinions of the Inland River Steamboat Industry Association

Representatives will be sent to Beijing to present in person for consideration and adoption.

Since the Minister of Communications, Yu Fei, convened a meeting in Shanghai to consult with private shipping merchants for opinions on reorganization, the Shanghai Inland River Steamboat Industry Association immediately selected members with rich shipping experience and knowledge to form a subcommittee to discuss and draft opinions through several meetings. The draft was submitted and approved by the 72nd Executive Committee meeting of the association and was officially submitted to the Ministry of Communications for review yesterday. The following is a summary of the main points of the opinion letter: 1. Regarding the registration of steamboat businesses, it is believed that separate laws and regulations for the management of the steamboat industry should be drafted first, and Article 3 of the Regulations on the Supervision of Public Utilities by Private Enterprises should be amended regarding the central and local supervisory authorities, to clarify the division of power between the central and local governments and facilitate the management of shipping affairs. 2. Regarding the reorganization of scheduled routes, it is believed that the Provisional Measures for Issuing Ship Route Permits should be abolished to eliminate existing disputes over routes. For ships operating on scheduled routes, the Ministry should issue scheduled passage certificates in accordance with Article 4, Paragraph 2 of the Maritime Law. For ships operating on unscheduled routes, the competent shipping administration bureau should issue temporary passage certificates, and operating standards should be established separately for both scheduled and unscheduled services. 3. Regarding promoting shipping cooperation, it is believed that the Ministry of Communications should prescribe steps and use administrative power to enforce them, and instruct local shipping organizations to organize joint operating bureaus or water fee systems among businesses operating on the same scheduled routes. If this proves ineffective, the Ministry should order businesses on the same route to merge and form organizations. 4. Regarding the addition of ships, it is believed that the Ministry's proposed principle is in line with the principles of improving tools for public utilities and should be supported. 5. Regarding encouraging the construction of new ships and the demolition of old ships, it is believed that it should be extended to small inland river vessels, and the Ministry of Communications should consult with the Ministry of Finance to allocate the stipulated subsidies in advance for application. 6. Regarding the adjustment of sailing schedules, it is believed that it should be handled with reference to the opinions on the reorganization of scheduled routes. Changes to schedules should be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval before implementation. 7. Regarding the supervision of freight rates and ticket prices, it is believed that the standards for supervision should be based on Article 12 of the Regulations on the Supervision of Public Utilities by Private Enterprises, and the Ministry of Communications should jointly form a Steamboat Industry Freight Review Committee with local shipping organizations and state-owned shipping agencies to be specifically responsible for the review and supervision of freight rates. 8. Regarding the supervision of operations, it is believed that a detailed item on the supervision of operations should be included in the Steamboat Industry Supervision Rules, and a special department for the supervision of operations should be added to the Shipping Administration Department, and the organizational law of the Shipping Administration Bureau should be revised to authorize local shipping administration bureaus to supervise the operations of the shipping industry and appoint experts with rich experience and knowledge to serve as supervisory officials in charge. In addition, the following suggestions were made regarding the current problems of the shipping industry: 1. Unify the administrative authority of shipping affairs to achieve the practical effect of reorganizing the shipping industry. 2. Recover and unify the administration of port affairs to facilitate the revitalization of the shipping industry. 3. Improve the ship inspection system to raise ship inspection standards. 4. Establish a training institute for crew members to promote navigation education. 5. Organize a shipping advisory committee to seek cooperation between shipping administration and merchants to collect ideas and broaden benefits. 6. Establish a transportation dispute arbitration committee to avoid illegal competition between railways, highways, and waterways. 7. Reorganize waterways and dredge rivers to facilitate the navigation of ships. 8. State-owned and private shipping industries should cooperate to resist the intrusion of foreign shipping and seek the development of national shipping. All the opinions and suggestions are very thorough in their arguments, pinpoint the current shortcomings of shipping administration, and are indeed necessary and urgent policies for shipping administration construction and shipping industry reorganization. The entire document is tens of thousands of words long, with precise opinions and fluent writing, making it an important resource for reorganizing the private shipping industry. It is reported that the association will send representatives to Beijing again when necessary to present detailed opinions on the reorganization of the shipping industry for reference by the transportation authorities.

Commodity Inspection: Raw Silk Inspection Conference Held Yesterday

Silk experts from the League of Nations attended to provide guidance; a proposal to revise the draft standard.

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce convened a silk industry conference of four provinces, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, and Sichuan, at the International Trade Bureau auditorium at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. More than 30 representatives, including Chu Hui-seng, Shen Chen, Huang Ji-wen, Qian Feng-gao, Cheng Bing-ruo, and Zhu Jing-an, attended. After the chairman, Miao Zhong-xiu, presided over the ceremony, the chairman reported, stating that the quality of raw silk exported from China is not uniform, and merchants often mix inferior quality silk for sale overseas. As a result, various countries have a poor impression of raw silk produced in China. To restore credibility, the bureau has specifically stipulated inspection methods for raw silk products. Then, the draft inspection standard was submitted. As a result of the discussion, the participating representatives believed that because the silk reeling machines used in China are outdated, it would be difficult to immediately improve the product standards and raise the standards to the level of the draft standard, and silk factories would be adversely affected. They proposed that the bureau revise the draft standard. Finally, two silk experts from the League of Nations, Mr. Manfield and Mr. Ma Yue, provided guidance on various methods related to sericulture, and the meeting adjourned.

Although not in danger... there is no major problem.

Huaping Steamer's Telegram Reports Rescue

It has been driven to Quanzhou to unload cargo yesterday.

The Huaping steamer of the Minxin Company, weighing 1,500 tons, loaded a large shipment of flour and groceries in Shanghai on the 18th of this month and sailed to Sizhou, Fujian. At about 2:00 p.m. on the 21st, it was sailing outside the port of Quanzhou when it was forced to hit a reef due to bad weather, difficult navigation, and rapid currents. After the accident, it telegraphed the Shanghai office to report and tried to get out of danger. According to the company yesterday, the ship was rescued yesterday morning (22nd) and has been driven to Quanzhou. It is currently unloading cargo. Whether there is damage to the bottom of the ship will be known after the cargo is unloaded and inspected. Because the bottom of the ship is double-layered, it can still sail after hitting a reef.

Public Health Development in the Past Four Years

Issued by the Municipal Government

The Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday released the public health development in the past four years, stating that the city government has added six clinics, three hospitals, one isolation hospital, multiple drug rehabilitation centers, and one health testing laboratory in the past four years, which can represent the general progress in public health. The health plan is divided into six items: 1. To improve the city's sanitation, inspect beverages and food, and clean streets and rivers. 2. To prevent the spread of epidemics, the implementation methods are: a. Free vaccination. b. Promote health education to make the general public aware of the importance of health. 3. To protect the health of the general public, such as stipulating the working hours and treatment of pregnant female workers, and investigating school health conditions. The other two plans are: 1. To conduct scientific analysis of the insulation problem in the testing laboratory. 2. To compile a household survey form. In addition, there is also a kind of work related to hygiene, which is the inspection of meat. As of the end of last year, a total of 450,100 dan of various types of meat were inspected. As a result, very little rotten meat was found on the market. The establishment of isolation hospitals is also one of the important health facilities. A total of 1,619 male patients and 1,277 female patients were treated in the past two years. Drug rehabilitation work is also one of the aspects of the city government's health plan. In the past four years, drug rehabilitation centers have been established in Nanshi, Zhabei, and Longhua, and a drug offender rehabilitation center has been established on Jinyi Road. The four drug rehabilitation centers have cured 7,006 drug addicts. The greatest success of the city government's health plan in the past four years is the construction of a municipal hospital, a health testing laboratory, and a medical school, all of which are nearing completion. The municipal hospital can currently accommodate 200 beds, and will be expanded to 2,000 to 3,000 beds in the future. The medical school can accommodate 300 students.

Zhu Xiongwu's Case of Soliciting Litigation: Trial Concluded, Sentencing Scheduled; Only One Witness, Xu, Appeared at the Trial Yesterday; Prosecutor Argued for Multiple Offenses to be Combined and Punished Severely; Dismissed Clerk of the Jiangsu High Court Was Placed

Zhu Xiongwu, a dismissed clerk of the Jiangsu High Court, was arrested and sent to the Wuxian District Court for defamation of the court president, Zhu Shusheng. During the investigation, it was discovered that Zhu Xiongwu had colluded with Chen Chao-zuan, another clerk of the court, and Lu Wenguang, a lawyer's clerk,

to solicit litigation and defraud people of money in as many as eight cases. The prosecuting prosecutor filed a public prosecution against Zhu et al., and the Supreme Court ruled that Zhu Xiongwu be transferred to the jurisdiction of the Shanghai First Special District Court. For the convenience of the trial, the Wuxian District Court sent Chen and Lu to Shanghai together with Zhu for a joint trial. Huang Risheng, a judge of the First Special Court, has held two court sessions, summoned witnesses, and interrogated them. Chen was released on bail of 500 yuan, and Zhu and Lu were remanded in custody pending further interrogation. All the details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, the third

trial was held. Only one witness, Xu, appeared. According to Xu, the Yutai Company in this city was collecting debts from the Zoucangtai Rice Mill in Wuxi. He testified about the situation during the mediation at Ji Yunqing's house in Wuxi, saying that Zhu Xiongwu was not present when the mediation agreement was written. Later, he saw Jiang Hongbin, a partner of Yutai Company, in the pavilion of Ji's house, but he did not talk to him at the time. Jiang testified in court earlier that after receiving the 5,000 yuan from Zou Cangtai, he gave 2,500 yuan to us as a reward, which was not true. However, Jiang told me on the train back to Shanghai that he would ask the manager after he got to the store

for instructions before rewarding us again, but so far there has been no action. The court then continued to interrogate the defendant Lu Wenguang about soliciting Li Shannan's appeal and demanding compensation from Li. Lu still pleaded guilty, saying that although Li's letter to him had such a tone, Li did not accuse me of soliciting in his previous testimony. The court decided to interrogate Chen Chaozuan about the reason for the phrase "special relationship" in his letter to Zhu Xiongwu. Chen admitted that it was

an inappropriate term at the time and had no other hidden meaning. Then, Zhu Xiongwu was repeatedly interrogated about his relationship with Jiang Hongbin, his motive for participating in the debt mediation between Yutai and Zou Cangtai, and the process. However, Zhu resolutely denied having taken such actions. He was also asked about the reason for communicating with Weng Jun. Zhu said that he could not remember because it had been many years. Finally, he was asked about the letter signed "Zhu Xinfu" to Lu Wenguang found in Lu's house. What case was mentioned in the letter? And what was the intention of the note written in Zhu's own handwriting, congratulating each other on getting rich, and addressing each other as brothers, which was also found in Lu's house? Zhu said that Lu's nephew, Ru Yide, had admitted in his previous testimony that it was a joke. As for the note, although it was my playful writing, I cannot be considered to have committed a crime by writing this note. The court pointed out that it had been verified that Zhu Xinfu, or Zhu Yi-wu, was Zhu Xiongwu's name, so Zhu Xinfu was also an alias of the defendant, and the envelope of the letter was from the Jiangsu High Court. Lu was Zhu's friend, and the letter was found in Lu's house, so it was definitely not Lu who

framed Zhu. He was ordered to state the whole story clearly, but Zhu always said that he did not know. Judge Huang stated that the evidence had been

investigated and ordered the debate to begin. The prosecutor then rose to argue, mainly stating that Zhu had colluded with the lawyer's clerk and communicated with each other. Although it is difficult to verify each of the points accused, the letters for reconciliation and requests for payment are enough to constitute the crimes of soliciting lawsuits, defrauding money, and dereliction of duty. The correspondence between Chen and Zhu leaked the news of the court's handling of the case. Lu's publicity has been found in several cases based on the evidence, and it can be inferred that there are more undiscovered cases. He should be punished severely for multiple offenses. Then, the defendant's lawyer gave his defense, saying that the results of the investigation were not sufficient to constitute the crimes charged. After the defense was completed, the court ordered Chen to pay the original bail, and Zhu and Lu were remanded in custody to await sentencing at 2:00 p.m. on the 29th of this month.

He immediately reported to Captain Zhang and assigned detectives Deng Shaochen and officers Li Wenjie and Liu Jianxiu from the Laobeimen Police Station to set up an ambush. At 6:30 PM, they intercepted the three robbers, Tong, Wu, and Jin. They confiscated a six-inch Browning pistol with six bullets and a fake pistol. They were taken to the station and, after a brief interrogation, handed over to the designated personnel for further questioning at the Bureau.

Prince Qing Sentenced to Twelve Years for Smuggling Drugs

Cui Chengyao, a Chinese detective from the Huishan Police Station, arrested Wang Ziqing, a resident of Haimen (38 years old), near Dalianwan Road and Kunming Road at around 9:00 PM on the sixth of this month for smuggling the drug red pills. Four packs of Sen pills, totaling 2,000 pills, wrapped in Japanese newspapers and cloth, with Japanese characters on the cloth, were found. Wang was taken to the police station and handed over to the First Special District Court for questioning. Wang testified that two Japanese men, whose names he did not know, gave him the red pills to deliver to a Chinese man near 547 Dalianwan Road, who was short and stout and holding a newspaper as a mark. He claimed that he only received one yuan for each delivery and that the pills were not his. The court adjourned the hearing. The main culprit could not be found. The defendant's testimony remained the same, and he pleaded for leniency. He was ordered to remain in custody pending judgment. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao presided over the court and sentenced Wang Ziqing to twelve years in prison, confiscating the evidence.

Fugitive Arrested in Zhejiang's Shizhai Village Robbery and Murder Case; Escorted to First Special District Court Yesterday Morning to Notify Zhejiang Provincial Court for Extradition

In 1933, five or six robbers broke into the home of the Shi family in Shizhai Village, Zhejiang Province, armed with weapons, and attempted to rob them. They opened fire, killing a woman named Zhu Chao and a girl named Shi Lan. After investigating the case, the Pujiang County Court of Zhejiang Province determined that Shi Limin, Shi Yufang, and Wu Xianbi, also known as Wu Hunshan, were related to the case and issued arrest warrants. Recently, the Zhejiang Provincial Public Security Bureau arrested Shi Limin and handed him over to the court for interrogation. Shi Limin confessed that his accomplice, Wu Xianbi, had fled. Until 9:15 PM the previous evening, Gao Wentai, a relative of the victim who worked at the Shanghai Shenxin No. 9 Factory, encountered Wu Xianbi on the road and secretly followed him. Gao saw Wu enter Room 12, Yong'an Lane, 1043 Tokyo Road. Gao reported this information to the Putuo Road Police Station, who dispatched detectives to arrest Wu Xianbi and detain him at the station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to Criminal Court Eight of the First Special Court. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin from the Police Station stated the background of the case and requested that Wu Xianbi be detained so that the Zhejiang Provincial Court could be notified to send personnel to extradite him. He also stated that the information reported by Gao Wentai was factual, but it had not yet been verified, and requested that he be released on bail. When questioned, Wu Xianbi claimed to have been a soldier in the army and had no knowledge of the robbery and murder case. Judge Tan ordered Wu to be detained and Gao Wentai to be released on bail.

Liu Qichang Sentenced to Six Months for Extortion; Acquitted of Charges Related to the Yangtze Hotel

Liu Changqi, the former manager of the Anlegong dance hall, and Wang Yaoxiang, Xue Qiyuan, and Zheng Daozhi were all friends. In January of this year, they jointly rented Room 106 of the Yuan Dong Hotel as a place of entertainment. At that time, Wang Yaoxiang was extremely fond of two courtesans, Er Nian and San Nian, from the Fengya brothel at 22 Huile Lane, and frequently called for them. On the 10th of that month, Zheng Daozhi also called for Fengya's Er Nian and San Nian at Room 547 of the Dongfang Hotel. When Liu Changqi and others learned of this, they believed that Zheng should not steal another's love, so they sent Xue Qiyuan, accompanied by Chai Yiqing and Cha Yiyuan, to Room 319 of the Dachina Hotel on the 13th to negotiate with Zheng, demanding that Zheng pay 50 yuan to settle the matter. Zheng only had 15 yuan on him at the time, which Xue and the others took away. However, Xue and the others were still not satisfied. The next day, they went to Room 704 of the Yangtze Hotel and robbed Zheng of his gold watch, worth over one hundred yuan. Zheng reported this to the Laozha Police Station, who ordered the detectives to arrest Xue, Chai, and Cha. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for trial. Xue was sentenced to nine months in prison, while Chai and Cha were acquitted. Liu Changqi had already fled. On the 14th of the month, at 1:20 AM, Chinese Detective Song Wenqing of the Laozha Police Station arrested Liu at the Far East Dance Hall and handed him over to the First Special Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, Criminal Judge Qian Hongye opened Criminal Court One for further hearings. Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang prosecuted Liu for extortion. When questioned, Liu Changqi denied extortion, claiming that he only demanded payment from Zheng Daozhi for debts owed to the Far East Company's room. The court then called Xue Qiyuan to the stand for identification. Although Xue had identified Liu as the person from his previous testimony at the police station, he suddenly claimed today that he did not know Liu. Liu also claimed that he did not know Xue. After Judge Qian reviewed the testimony, he sentenced Liu in court to six months in prison for extortion, acquitting him of the charges related to the Yangtze Hotel.

Public Concession May Crime Statistics

According to the Public Concession Police Department's May report, the reported crime cases within the concession this month totaled 1,854, an increase of 166 cases compared to April, and an increase of 411 cases compared to the same month last year. The number of criminals arrested also increased compared to the previous month and the same month last year, totaling 1,699 people. Among them, 108 people were arrested this month for crimes committed in previous months, and 87 people were arrested at the request of other government offices.

In terms of the types of crimes, there were five murder cases, six attempted murder cases, and twenty-six armed robbery cases this month, all fewer than the previous month and the same month last year. There were fifty-seven theft cases, fifty-four cases of home invasion, and twenty-two shop robbery cases reported in Group A this month, with twenty-three bandits captured. There were one hundred and twenty-nine pickpocketing cases, with one hundred and eight pickpockets captured. The number of stolen items included eighty-seven bicycles and one car. One car and seventeen bicycles were recovered, and eighteen bicycle thieves were captured. In addition, there were sixty-one snatching cases, with fifty-nine snatchers captured. According to statistics, the total property loss due to theft this month amounted to more than 83,000 yuan, and the recovered items were worth slightly less than 20,000 yuan.

Regarding the prohibition of smoking within the Public Concession, there were fifteen opium cases investigated by the Central Police Station this month, with sixty-nine opium offenders captured. Seventy-eight cases were reported and investigated by various police stations, with one hundred and seventy-nine opium offenders captured. Among them, one hundred and seventy-three were sentenced to imprisonment, seven were fined, twenty-eight were detained, one was sent back to the higher authorities, and the rest were released.

This month, there were two thousand eight hundred and eighty-four traffic violations, with seven hundred and fifteen prosecutions, including six hundred and thirty-four Chinese and eighty-one foreigners. The rest were either warned or had their violations recorded. There were three hundred and twenty-seven cases of excessive horn honking, with ninety-seven people convicted, including eighty-nine Chinese and eight foreigners. The licenses of three rickshaw pullers were revoked for excessive horn honking. There were two thousand and forty-three violations by public rickshaw pullers. The licenses of eighteen self-owned rickshaw pullers were revoked for soliciting customers. There were eight hundred and fifty-two cases of car accidents causing injury or damage, including eighty-eight cases of both damage and injury, one hundred and seventy-six cases of damage only, and two hundred and eighty-eight cases of injury only. Issued by the Shanghai Municipal Council Information Office.

Last Month, the Public Concession Parks Were Extremely Crowded

According to the Shanghai Municipal Council Parks Department's May report, the total number of visitors to various parks and children's playgrounds this month was 578,415, exceeding the number for the same month last year by more than 181,000. Furthermore, according to the report from the Jiaozhou Road Park Meteorological Testing Station, the total rainfall this month was 3.49 inches, the highest temperature was 80.1 degrees, the lowest was 47.4 degrees, the average high temperature was 70 degrees, and the average low temperature was 59.2 degrees. In addition, the construction of various park projects, the planting and transplantation of flowers and trees, etc., all proceeded smoothly. Moreover, a thatched pavilion has been added deep within the trees in the Brahma King Ferry Park, providing space for more than 400 people to stand, truly benefiting those who visit the park in the rain.

Therefore, it has been actively arranged and researched and prepared for more than half a year. The skin and flesh of the whole body are transparent like glass, hence the name. When swimming, you can see the skeleton of the whole body, and the blood vessels of the buttocks are reflected by the light, which is more clear and spectacular. In the dance hall, the Sidda Company has been hired to install scientific cold air this year. Its power is very strong and can dissipate the heat in the room and input fresh air from the outside. People in the hall not only do not feel the sultry heat, but also feel the cool breeze rising from the ground, which is more comfortable than in the suburbs. The windows are wide open, without the disadvantages of congestion and depression. It is more hygienic than the cold air methods of ammonia ice, etc.

Detailed Explanation of Postal Issues Published. The China Postal Workers Correspondence School, established by the Shanghai National Postal Workers Union, is not only committed to cultivating postal talents, but also publishes postal book series for reference by those interested in serving the postal industry and the community. One type that has been published is "Detailed Explanation of Postal Issues." The book was compiled by Mr. Gu Xizhang, a postal knowledge teacher at the school. The book is divided into six chapters, including 320 postal issues, which are analyzed, categorized, and explained in detail. The writing is simple and the wording is popular. The previous and subsequent issues are seamlessly connected. After reading this book, the entire postal system can be seen at a glance. Postal colleagues can read it as a postal dictionary. Those taking the postal exam can read it as a test guide. Modern citizens can read it as postal knowledge. At the end of the book, various postal laws and regulations are attached, which are essential reference materials for postal colleagues and those taking the postal exam. The whole book is hardcover, with more than 200 pages, and the price is 50 cents. Postal colleagues and students of the school can purchase it at a 20% discount. Those who purchase 10 copies in whole will be treated the same way. For out-of-town mail purchases, send them directly to the school at No. 9, Lane 538, Laobazi Road, Shanghai. Postage stamps can be used instead of foreign money, with full value, and no postage will be charged.

Sports News

Our National World Games Football Team: European Tour Miscellany – June 12th, Letter from Li Huitang in Medan

Closing Act: Harmony Prevails

June 5th marked the final match of our team's Java leg. The opponent was the Batavia’s Qunli Youth team, a combined team of two Chinese teams. After our victory over the league leaders with a score of 7-2 yesterday, our athletes felt quite fatigued despite their best efforts. Today, as one big family, there was no fierce competition. We arranged for those who were tired to have a rest, fielding the following lineup:

(That day at 11:00 AM, the Guangzhao Association held a welcome and farewell meeting, with the reporter offering thanks.)

Bao Jiaping, Tan Jiangbai, Mai Shaohan, Li Guowei, Liang Rongzhao, Zhang Xianyuan, Yang Shuiyi, Zhuo Shijin, Sun Jinshun, Huang Meishun, Jia Youliang

The first half ended 0-0, with the final score being 3-0. Jiangbai scored twice, and Jingxiang once.

This match was an internal affair. Although it was our team's final performance, the audience was sparse. The players were very polite, and the game was not tense at all. It is not surprising that the stands were deserted. Our team's performance in the first half was mediocre, resulting in a lack of highlights. In the second half, Li Tiansheng replaced Tan Jiangbai, and Wang Bai and Jingxiang were moved to the front line to replace Jinshun and Shijin. The forward line became more lively after this change, with Jiangbai and Jingxiang scoring successively. The opponent's skills were unremarkable. Even Li Yuxin, whom we considered promising and who had been selected to participate in the preliminary rounds, did not demonstrate any exceptional ability. Although our team's defense was not particularly strong, it was more than adequate. In the end, we won 3-0, concluding our Java tour with a record of ten wins and one draw.

This kind of record was previously achieved by South China in 1931. Our team's tour of Java this time possessed greater strength and should have achieved even more. However, due to the tight schedule, the hot weather, and unfavorable terrain, our true abilities could not be fully displayed. Moreover, to test our formation, the lineup was changed in every match, which slightly affected our teamwork. We only considered ourselves satisfied with three or four of the eleven performances in Java. However, in the dozen or so trials after leaving the country, although we made some sacrifices at the time, we did discover some of our own weaknesses, which was still valuable. As for impressions outside of the matches, this time we arrived and left in a hurry at each stop, like viewing flowers from horseback, and we didn’t really see anything much. The most obvious thing was the overseas Chinese compatriots’ very eager expectations for us. That's all. The reporter hopes to write a special article about the details of football in Java within ten days, which I'm afraid will be something domestic fans will enjoy reading.

Five-Hour Flight

After concluding our Java matches on June 5th, all the overseas Chinese organizations in Batavia held a farewell banquet that night at the Great Eastern Restaurant. The toasting and revelry reached a climax. After Consul-General Song gave his speech, Rong Jun and the reporter responded with thanks. The next morning, in order to make it to Singapore for the match against the Army-Navy Combined team on the 7th (Sunday), our team selected thirteen players, led by Director Rong, to fly to Singapore on a special plane. The remaining players would take a ship this afternoon to meet them in Singapore and then travel to Medan together. The selected players for the flight were Bao Jiaping, Li Tiansheng, Tan Jiangbai, Liang Rongzhao, Xu Yahui, Chen Zhenhe, Li Guowei, Cao Guicheng, Feng Jingxiang, Ye Beihua, Zheng Jiliang, and Huang Meishun. At 5:00 AM, after washing up, they drove to the airport. Dawn was just breaking, and the plane took off. Among these fourteen people, only Guowei and Jiliang were first-timers. Guowei was very curious, asking questions incessantly, while Jiliang's heart was pounding like a deer, trembling with fear. The whole team teased them all the more. Yahui and Xiao Heitan (Little Black Coal), with their aviation student qualifications, lectured and pointed, explaining the use of the instruments with great interest. After takeoff, they looked down at the cities and mountains, as clear as in a picture book. Sometimes, they looked down at the sea of clouds, which was a magnificent sight. When the plane passed over South Sumatra, they saw dense forests, endless as far as the eye could see. After five hours in the air, they landed safely at the Singapore airport at 11:05 AM, safely passing another dangerous moment. They drove back to the New Asia Hotel to rest and prepare for the fierce battle tomorrow.

Four Goose Eggs Given to the Army-Navy Combined Team

Although our team defeated the Singapore Selection with a score of 4-0 last month, everyone believed that the Singapore Selection's strength this year was mediocre, and our victory was not unexpected. Moreover, the victory came too easily, and it was regrettable that they could not see our team's brilliant performance. Therefore, they encouraged the football authorities to select the Army-Navy Combined team to compete against us when our team passed through Singapore again. The Army-Navy Combined team has several strong divisions, selecting the best of the best, making their force even greater. When two heroes meet, they are bound to awaken the fans' senses. The authorities complied with the public's wishes, and the match was held on the 7th (Sunday). For a time, fans from various cities outside of Singapore rushed to get there, traveling long distances. The authorities, mindful of the excessive crowding of fans in the previous match and the difficulty in maintaining order (one fan died from being squeezed), took precautions this time, limiting the capacity to 16,000 people, and refusing entry to anyone over that number. The seriousness of the situation was evident. Afterwards, it was heard that two hours before the start of the match on that day, the stadium was already completely surrounded, demonstrating the great appeal of the match. Our team used the same lineup that defeated the Batavia league leaders 7-2, except for Bao replacing Huang as goalkeeper.

Bao Jiaping, Tan Jiangbai, Li Tiansheng, Chen Zhenhe, Xu Yahui, Liang Rongzhao, Zheng Jiliang, Ye Beihua, Li Huitang, Feng Jingxiang, Cao Guicheng

The first half ended 2-0, with the final score being 4-0. Jingxiang, Guicheng, Beihua, and Huitang each scored once.

The Army-Navy Combined team was strong and powerful, with each player being enormous. Their appearance during practice gave us a great sense of threat. The match started at 5:00 PM. The other side passed the ball immediately upon receiving it, never stopping. This kind of sweeping, hacking strategy made us worry about how to respond for the first fifteen minutes. The opponent's crosses from the wings were accurate, and the center forward was over six feet tall. Their headers on goal were very dangerous. Fortunately, Bao and Tan defended with all their might, preventing a loss. In the 17th minute, Jingxiang received a low pass from Jiliang, scoring the first goal. Guicheng followed up with another goal, making the score 2-0 in the first half. After switching sides, our attack became even more intense. The opposing defenders and goalkeeper were overwhelmed, unable to defend everything. The reporter and Beihua successively scored two more goals, giving four goose eggs to the Army-Navy Combined team, earning unanimous praise from Chinese and foreign spectators. The overseas Chinese were even more delighted. Those who bet on our victory were overjoyed. The power of victory and its effects are truly incredible. Our team used this formation on that day because we considered it our strongest lineup and did not want to change it. Their understanding and coordination are becoming more and more perfect. It is commendable that the defense was able to keep a clean sheet, not conceding a single goal. It was also not easy for the sharp forwards to break through the opponent's tight defense and score four goals. We are even more convinced that this formation is the strongest one we have discovered. We are even more convinced that we must feel satisfied with the measures taken to make the football field soft and level. From the recent performances, it is even more certain that we are soft when we encounter soft, and even harder when we encounter hard.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Decides to Subsidize Half the Cost of Physics, Chemistry, and Biology Equipment for Secondary Schools – Funding of 500,000 Yuan Borne by Four Agencies

The Ministry of Education previously issued an order last year requiring public and private universities to establish research institutes. It has now decided to subsidize half the cost of physics, chemistry, and biology equipment for secondary schools nationwide. The subsidy funds will be borne equally by the China Education and Culture Foundation, the Board of Directors of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund, the Academia Sinica, and the Ministry of Education. The order will be implemented gradually from the next fiscal year. The equipment will be manufactured by the Instrument Workshop of the Institute of Physics of the Academia Sinica. The number of items to be manufactured in the first step is as follows: 1. 2,000 sets of physics experiment equipment for junior high schools; 2. 660 sets of physics demonstration equipment for junior high schools; 3. 660 sets of chemistry demonstration equipment for junior high schools; 4. 180 sets of physics demonstration equipment for senior high schools; 5. Continued production of 80 sets of physics experiment equipment for senior high schools; 6. 180 sets of chemistry demonstration equipment for senior high schools; 7. 3,600 sets of chemistry experiment equipment for senior high schools; 8. 900 sets of biology microscopes, etc. The chemical glassware will be planned by the Institute of Engineering. The instrument section has already started and requires 900,000 yuan.

This City's Joint Examination Started Yesterday – Director Pan Personally Inspected – Good Order in All Examination Venues

The joint graduation examination for secondary and normal schools in this city for the second semester of the 24th year has started yesterday in various school examination venues. Over 5,000 people are participating, and the order in each examination venue is good. Director Pan personally inspected and gave instructions on everything. The details are recorded as follows:

Number of Participants

There are 72 senior high schools, 3 senior high normal schools, 119 junior high simple normal schools, 1 kindergarten normal school, and schools participating this session, totaling 5,000 people. The examinations are held in the original examination venues. The Education Bureau will send personnel to conduct spot checks for junior high schools today and the last day. For those not spot-checked, the schools will conduct their own graduation examinations. There are subject in this session. The joint examination reward and punishment measures have been abolished.

Strict Supervision

The number of examination venues has increased this time, so the Education Bureau has sent a large number of staff and elementary school principals to serve as chief and co-supervisors, going to various venues to supervise each other. Candidates must present their admission tickets to enter the venue, and seats are arranged in advance. All examination papers are sealed. The chief supervisor will open and distribute them according to number on the spot. After the examination, the examination papers will be collected and sealed again by the chief supervisor, stamped with their private seal, and brought back to the Education Bureau for the Joint Examination Committee to grade and record the scores. The committee will then open the seal and verify the names. The process is very strict.

Good Order

Yesterday, Director Pan personally inspected the examination venues and gave instructions on everything. The students in the examination venues were buried in their papers, with high spirits and good order. The staff of the Joint Examination Committee are stationed at the Huguang Society, working late into the night, very tense.

Today's Subjects

Senior high school: Mathematics from 8:30 AM to 11:30 AM; Foreign Language from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM. Junior high school: Mathematics from 8:30 AM to 10:30 AM; Foreign Language from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM. Senior high normal school: Mathematics from 8:30 AM to 11:30 AM; Elementary School Teaching Materials and Education Law from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM. Kindergarten normal school: Childcare Law from 8:30 AM to 11:30 AM; Kindergarten Teaching Materials and Education Law from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM. The examinations will conclude today.

Henan Provincial Government Seeks Opportunities for Graduates: Approves Measures for Improving Vocational Education and Internship Opportunities for Graduates

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Henan Provincial Government, recognizing that in recent years there has been a large number of Henan and Jiangxi graduates from vocational schools of all levels inside and outside the province, and that their skills are either not being utilized or there are no places to utilize them, which is a great loss to the state's original intention of cultivating talent, has decided to take measures to expand the opportunities for vocational school graduates in order to remedy this situation. The Department of Education was first instructed to draft appropriate measures, and then, together with the Finance Department and the Secretariat, to carefully investigate and revise them. The following are the "Henan Provincial Government's Measures for Improving Vocational Education" and "Henan Provincial Government's Measures for Internship Opportunities for Vocational School Graduates," which were approved at the provincial government meeting on the 16th and promulgated for implementation:

Measures for Improving Vocational Education

The Provincial Government, in order to improve vocational education, cultivate vocational talent, and promote the development of social industries, hereby stipulates these measures. In order to ensure that the facilities and plans of vocational schools meet the needs of social industries in this province and the administrative plans of various departments of this province, the Department of Education shall consult with the various departments to jointly determine them. When various departments and subordinate agencies of this Provincial Government need certain types of talent, they should consult with the Department of Education at any time to establish the relevant vocational schools or add the relevant vocational courses to cultivate them. The various departments and subordinate agencies of this Provincial Government may consult with the Department of Education to unify talent cultivation when organizing various vocational training classes. When various departments and subordinate agencies of this Provincial Government need vocational talent, they may give priority to selecting vocational school graduates or hold public examinations to provide vocational students with equal opportunities. The various departments and subordinate agencies of this Provincial Government may provide internship opportunities for vocational schools to enhance their skills and service capabilities (the internship measures and budget will be determined separately). The various departments and subordinate agencies of this Provincial Government should comply with the orders of the central government and provide vocational schools with practical opportunities to compensate for the lack of school equipment and gain practical experience (the practical measures will be determined separately). These measures may be revised at any time if there are any omissions. These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Measures for Internship Opportunities for Vocational Students

These measures are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the "Henan Provincial Government's Measures for Improving Vocational Education." Any graduates of provincial, county, and approved private vocational schools, universities, and vocational departments in this province who volunteer to participate in internships should fill out an internship application form and submit it to the Department of Education for registration by the original school from June 1st to July 15th of each year. Interns who have registered and passed the review will be assigned to various internships by the provincial government. The review, selection, and assignment of interns will be handled by the Henan Provincial Government's Vocational School Graduates Internship Committee (the committee's regulations will be determined separately). Once an intern has been assigned to an internship institution, they may not request a change of assignment. Internship institutions are limited to the various departments and subordinate agencies of the provincial government. The internship period is six months, but it may be extended or shortened when necessary. Interns should obey the orders of the leaders of the internship institutions, abide by all rules, and serve faithfully. Interns shall not leave their posts without permission. In case of special circumstances, they must submit a request to the leader of the internship institution for approval. Those who leave their posts without approval may have their internships terminated. During the internship period, each intern will be given a monthly living allowance: 8 yuan for junior students, 12 yuan for senior students, and 16 yuan for university students. Those with excellent internship performance may receive a moderate increase. The internship performance will be evaluated by the provincial government, which will issue evaluation methods to the leaders of the internship institutions, who will be responsible for the evaluation and report it for record during the internship period. Upon completion of the internship, interns should prepare an internship report and submit it to the leader of the internship institution for forwarding to the provincial government for record. Interns with particularly outstanding internship performance will be employed by the internship institutions if possible, and will also be kept on file by the provincial government for future use. These measures may be revised at any time if there are any omissions. These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (End)

Overview of the National Provincial and Municipal Normal School Student Graduation Examinations for the 23rd Year of the Republic

The Ministry of Education recently compiled statistics on the graduation examinations of normal school students in various provinces and cities across the country. The following is a summary:

(Explanation) Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Guangdong, Yunnan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Chahar, Gansu, Beijing, and Shanghai are all in the second semester. Qinghai and Hebei are all in the first semester. Jiangxi and Qingdao are not divided into first and second semesters. The rest are the sum of the first and second semesters. Among the 373 schools, there are 147 normal schools, 37 rural normal schools, 139 simplified rural normal schools, and 12 kindergarten normal schools. Among the 12,555 students participating, there are 5,745 from normal schools, 956 from rural normal schools, 4,534 from simplified normal schools, 1,058 from simplified rural normal schools, and 262 from kindergarten normal schools. Among the 7,340 students who passed, there are 3,941 from normal schools, 491 from rural normal schools, 2,060 from simplified normal schools, 689 from simplified rural normal schools, and 159 from kindergarten normal schools. Among the total number of passing students, 6,832 passed the regular normal school examinations, and 508 passed the supplementary examinations. In terms of percentage, the percentage of passing students out of participating students is 68.60% for normal schools, 51.36% for rural normal schools, 45.43% for simplified normal schools, 65.12% for simplified rural normal schools, and 60.69% for kindergarten normal schools, with a total average of 58.46%.

Multi-Party Profit Taking Halts Cotton Price Surge

The cotton market experienced a morning decline followed by an afternoon rise, ultimately resulting in a flat outcome. However, overseas cotton markets in India and America continued their dramatic upward trend. Due to the large-scale profit-taking by local investors the cotton market has appeared relaxed. Market prices have reversed downwards. The bullish investors are abandoning the current month and rolling over to July contracts, suggesting that spot cotton is extremely tight.

**Headline:** Near Month Drops, Far Month Rises

Before the opening of the spot cotton market, American cotton continued to rise by nine to sixteen points, Indian cotton continued its steep upward trend increasing by 2.5 to 3.5 rupees, and Osaka cotton rose by 5.6 sen. Before the market opened, market sentiment was unanimously bullish. Unexpectedly, a large number of profit-taking investors seized the opportunity to sell, loosening supply and causing the market to reverse downwards. As a result, all months experienced a drop of 3.5 sen compared to the previous day's close, and new cotton fell by 5 sen. After the afternoon opening, because bullish investors continued to take profits, the market appeared weak. By the third close, it suddenly turned strong, and as the news for American cotton remained optimistic, short sellers also came to cover their positions. The market situation shifted from flat to tight. As a result, all months experienced an increase of 0.5 to 4.5 sen compared to the morning closing price, and new cotton rose by 5 sen to 1 sen, with the exception of the current month falling by 2.5 sen. Sales included Changhe 11,100 bales, Yuanxingchang 5,600 bales, Jinkang 3,500 bales, Yongda 2,000 bales, Shengyuan 2,800 bales, Yuanyi 4,500 bales, Renfeng 2,600 bales, Shenji 5,100 bales, Daji 2,800 bales, Dafu 2,500 bales, and Mingde 4,300 bales. Purchases included Xincheng 7,500 bales, Dachang 3,400 bales, Runkang 8,800 bales, Changfeng 8,100 bales, Yichang 2,900 bales, Hexing 6,800 bales, Yuda 3,200 bales, Xing 3,400 bales, Dafeng 1,100 bales, and Xingchang 1,700 bales. The market for patterned fabrics has already risen, but market prices are still flat. Purchases from various gangs are good. Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Fang Zheng)

If we were to compare the love of young people to white sugar and plums, that would be most appropriate. However, many young people refuse to eat plums one after another. They only know that when they experience a broken heart, they commit suicide, jump into the river, and do all sorts of shocking and tragic things. They do not know their own value, which is ten thousand times greater than a plum! Friends who are heartbroken! Please think twice before you act.

Although love is an indispensable process during youth, one must not become obsessed with it. Because many promising young people have an enterprising spirit in whatever career they pursue before they fall in love. Once they have a lover, they not only stop seeking career advancement, but also indulge in pink dreams all day long, and their ambitions decline. It is truly lamentable! Therefore, love can easily affect our future. May all young people in the world pay attention to this.

About the Grand View Garden Model

— Ya Chang

Ms. Yang Lingfu's handmade model of the Grand View Garden in the Summer Palace is exquisite and natural. All the pavilions, terraces, winding railings, and rooms, the rugged rocks, the lush vegetation, and the garden scenery are all lifelike, making people yearn for it as if they were there. Ms. Yang is truly a person with unique ingenuity. Ms. Yang began working on the Grand View Garden model when she was in her teens. After the Grand View Garden model was completed in 1919, she took it to various places for public exhibition. At that time, Ms. Yang wrote an article about the Grand View Garden model, narrating its construction from beginning to end. I recently found this article in old notes while sorting through my belongings, so I transcribed it here to enrich Spring and Autumn.

"When I made the Grand View Garden, I had never read the entire Dream of the Red Chamber. When I was eight or nine years old, I loved the Six Principles of Painting but had no teacher. I heard people say that learning to paint must start with boundary painting. Li Chengqiu of the Song Dynasty and Qiu Shifu of the Ming Dynasty were masters of exquisite buildings, and no one has succeeded them since. There happened to be a complete map of the Grand View Garden on the wall, so I copied it day and night. However, my love for architecture is even greater than my love for painting. Even during times of chaos and hasty escape, I always carried my tools with me. In my spare time from reading, I built small houses with diligence. In 1919, I took out what I had made over the years and kept the best ones, getting five or six kinds of pavilions and terraces. I wanted to build a garden, but I had no drawings, so I imitated the Grand View Garden that I had copied as a child. At that time, I knew the origins of the Grand View Garden from the Dream of the Red Chamber. Dream of the Red Chamber is a masterpiece of fiction. Since I built this garden, I had to match it with the origins of the garden, so I read Dream of the Red Chamber. After reading it, I greatly regretted it, saying: the people in Dream of the Red Chamber are all people I have often seen. Young masters from relatives like Jia Baoyu are abundant. There are many young ladies in the world who are depressed and suffering like Lin Daiyu. The other people are opportunistic and despicable, people whom I avoid whenever possible. So there is nothing to take from the people or the events. The only thing to take is their writing style. Why would I plan it and build it, to build a palace for those people? That is really devoting too much effort. Since my garden mistakenly uses the name of the Grand View Garden, people will definitely say that I am deeply familiar with the Redology and worship its book, so I narrate its origins like this."

Shiyu Anecdotes

— Qing Qu

Shiyu (shad) is available in late spring and early summer, not at other times, so it was originally called "Shiyu" (seasonal fish). People added a radical to the character for fish to specialize it, but it is actually a vulgar character. This fish has an elegant and flat shape, similar to bream but longer. It is no more than three feet long, and its scales dazzle the eye. When it first comes out of the water, it is as white as silver, different from ordinary fish. According to the fishermen, "When the fish are caught in a net, all the other fish jump and try to escape, but this fish is silent and motionless, for fear of damaging its scales." And those who love to eat it also value its fat in the scales, so when steamed, they consider the scales the supreme delicacy.

But the flesh has many thorns, as fine as hair, so the ancients listed it as one of the five regrets. The so-called "I know to love myself, only the scales are good, difficult to satisfy with sentiment are the many thorns," is not false. However, reciting "Do not hate the skinny bones that are difficult to search, it is okay to chew with the silver scales," is for those who know the taste to appreciate, and a boor chewing with a full mouth, resulting in a bone stuck in the throat, unable to spit it out or stay easy, is not the fault of the fish, but the fault of not knowing how to eat it. Because its rich texture is in the scales, it is suitable for clear stewing, which melts when heated, and the soup is unparalleled, so it is a delicacy of early summer, which lies in this.

It spawns between fresh water and sea water, with Fuchun River in Zhejiang being the most famous. Jiangyin, Jiangsu, is also quite famous. When it first enters the market, its price is extremely high. In my county, it comes from Shidong in Songjiang. This year, it was seen in the market close to the Start of Summer, which can be said to be the latest. But its value is still expensive, and only the wealthy and those with a gluttonous addiction dare to inquire about it. The other day, a certain family had a wedding banquet with this dish, bought from Shanghai to treat the guests, but the waiters did not recognize it. By the time the guests had finished eating and the plate was brought up, many had not had a chance to taste it. This has become a talking point, adding a new record to the humorous history of eating "Shiyu."

When the Pomegranate Flowers Bloom

— Zhou Qifeng

The pomegranate flowers are blooming,

Blooming so brightly and brilliantly, like fire.

One, two, three plants are connected, the flowers are so many and so red, densely crowded together, looking from a distance, like a large red satin unfurled in the sky.

The early summer wind, lazy and drunk, as if mixed with a lot of alcohol, sweeps through the city, sweeps through the fields, sweeps through the fiery pomegranate flowers, sweeps through the scattered couples of men and women under the pomegranate flowers.

Frenzied laughter, whispered sweet nothings, sweet songs, intertwined with the fragrance of powder, light cheongsam corners, men's pointed-toe leather shoes, constitute a sketch of modern bourgeois youth life. No pain, no sorrow, no worry, the world seems to exist for them, the pomegranate flowers seem to bloom for them.

The man is always humble, always reciting like a formula:

"Darling, you are the driving force of my life, without you, I cannot live... Yes, everything I have belongs to you, every cell, every..."

The woman pouted as usual, looking impatient, and after the man had rambled on for a long time, she turned her head slightly and blurted out three words:

"How annoying!"

However, in the woman's heart, there was no response of "How annoying," she was still the "driving force" of the man's life. Under the pomegranate flowers, everyone smoothly completed their own romance.

The pomegranate flowers are blooming,

Blooming so brightly and brilliantly, like fire! But it cannot awaken the numb hearts of pleasure-seekers!

Zongzi

— Ou

The weather is so sultry. It's hard to even breathe in the house, and sweat flows like tree sap, sticking to all our clothes, as if we've grown another layer of skin. The children are all irritable. Only mother is an exception. This kind of humid weather seems to have no effect on her at all. She's still running around in the front and back yards as usual, helping the old maid who has been with our family for fourteen years with all the housework. When she gets tired, she'll at most pick up a cup of cold tea and take a sip, then rush off to do things again.

The day after my ninth brother and I put on our bamboo cloth gowns, Grandfather sent someone from the shop with two baskets of loquats (we didn't know at the time if they were red-fleshed or white-fleshed). After we had eaten one basket by robbing, stealing, and deceiving, we suddenly thought of the zongzi that we always had every year, and we thought that zongzi should be eaten at the same time as loquats. So, regardless of how busy Mother was, we kept pestering her to make zongzi. That year, Grandmother happened to be sick in bed, and besides managing the household affairs as usual, Mother also had to take care of Grandmother's medicine, so she was really busy enough. In addition, the old maid who had been with our family for fourteen years walked slowly, and it always took her more than an hour to come back every time she went to the street. She went to the street three times a day, so she spent most of her time on the street, leaving only Mother to be busy at home.

But she was determined not to deprive us of our right to eat zongzi this year. She finally took the time out of her busy schedule to wrap many meat zongzi and red bean paste zongzi for us. Of course, she didn't have time during the day, so she wrapped these zongzi late into the night. When we got up the next morning and rushed to ask the old maid to unwrap the zongzi for us to eat, Mother sat lazily on a bamboo chair, watching us with a bitter smile. The old maid asked her if she wanted her to unwrap one for her too, but she just shook her head. After we walked out the door with our schoolbags, I seemed to hear Mother vomiting. Ninth Brother didn't understand and whispered to me, "Mother must have eaten too many zongzi last night." I was a few years older than him, and although I knew that his guess was wrong, I couldn't imagine how hard she had worked for us.

When I came home at noon, Mother's neck was covered with red, black scraped marks, and she hadn't even eaten yet. When Ninth Brother saw that half of the zongzi basket was gone (it had been taken to give away), he wanted to lose his temper, but I quickly held him back.

This was already eighteen or nineteen years ago, but every time I eat zongzi around the Dragon Boat Festival, it is bound to reappear on the screen of my mind.

The Fallen Flowers of Yingzhou, a recent work by the seaside fisherman, with profound meaning, has been widely distributed. Thank you for sending me a copy from Shanghai Shandong Road Social Book Bureau.

A New Couple

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: The Rain and Wind Still Leave Traces; The Night is Quiet and the Heart Pens a Letter of Severance

Miss Jiang was not as shockingly surprised as the last time I saw her. She slowly walked to my side, a faint smile appearing on her face. This faint smile could only be discerned from the slight movement of the corners of her mouth and the slight shift of her dark eyes. When she was more than ten paces away, she was always slightly lowering her head, waiting until she was within ten paces, then she would lower her eyelids. In this process of the faint smile, I had one of my clearest understandings, and I even raised my hand to take off my hat and salute her. But when my hand reached the brim of my hat, I felt a bit reckless, and I did not have the courage to take off my hat, so I lowered my hand again. But when I was touching the brim of my hat, a faint smile was also faintly revealed on my face. The other person saw this faint smile, and she accepted my gesture in a very calm manner, and did not think that my action was out of the ordinary. After this encounter, if I were five years younger, I would have jumped a few times in the alley. Now, although it was inconvenient to jump up, I felt that my steps were much lighter. With these opportunities, I released the irrepressible emotions in my heart. The second time, she very clearly sent a faint smile to me. She was already within a pace of me, and although she saw it very clearly, she was not shy in the least. She glanced at me quickly, and then lowered her head and left. The third time, I had some courage, and I still raised my hand and touched the brim of my hat, as if I were about to nod my head. Miss Jiang's faint smile also changed a bit under such social circumstances. When it flickered at the corners of her mouth, it already revealed two rows of neat white teeth. It was clear that she was smiling deeply. About two days passed with this touching of the hat brim in salute and a deep smile in response. My mother, Mrs. Zhang, was a little surprised. When I went to eat lunch with her, Mrs. Zhang looked at my face and asked, "Child, have you been preoccupied these past few days?" I lowered my head and ate, answering, "No." Mrs. Zhang said, "That can't be. When you are home, you are either writing or reading. These past few days, when you go to school, you are always looking at your watch, afraid of being late. When you come home, you seem to have found something valuable, and your face is full of smiles. But you can't sit still, you are just wandering around in the study, and lying in bed, as if there is a happy thing that you can't settle down with. Today is Sunday, you don't have to go to teach. But you are still often looking at your watch, and you run out in a hurry. After you run out, you come back smiling." I laughed, "Mom is asking about this matter. This matter is indeed ridiculous. I forgot that today was Sunday, and I hurried to school. When I got there, I saw that there was no one there, and I realized that it was Sunday, so I came back smiling." (38)

Wanderings

From Slender West Lake to Four Five Six

— Ai Mei

Wandering for several years, my footsteps have not yet left the province of Jiangsu; moreover, the places I've been to are either bustling metropolises or impoverished backwaters like living hells. If I were to reluctantly name a scenic spot that's more worthy of my longing, it would only be the Slender West Lake in Yangzhou. However, I've been separated from it for two years now! Truly: My body is covered in the dust of the world, I'm ashamed to say!

This trip to Yangzhou had two purposes: — First, of course, was to explore the beauty of the long-missed Slender West Lake; Second, was to visit the renowned Women's Life Class attached to the Provincial Yangzhou Middle School, which I had long heard of. Unfortunately, with only three nights, I was constantly attending gatherings, how annoying! Fortunately, the second day's gathering, besides the meal, included a lake tour, so I didn't entirely waste the trip; but I ultimately failed to visit the Women's Life Class, which is indeed a regret of this trip.

It was a clear and sunny afternoon, and I, along with Zhou and Zhu, strolled out of the North Gate, heading towards the lake. Along the way, a gentle breeze caressed our faces, and the bright sun enveloped us; truly! In this time of late spring and early summer, the afternoon weather was indeed very comfortable.

Upon reaching Green Willow Village, we were surrounded by boatmen; but the famed boat girls were nowhere to be seen. This was naturally because we were too late. We looked at the sky and realized it was indeed late, so we decided to visit only Little Gold Mountain and Xu Garden. As the ancients said, "Whether climbing mountains or crossing water, one must always leave some places unvisited, so as to allow for longing; otherwise, I would feel that my interest has been exhausted." We were very convinced by this famous saying. So, we boarded the boat we had hired. — Speaking of the boat, it was very simple, with only a white cloth awning on top and three rattan chairs below, barely enough to accommodate us!

With a punt pushing off from the lake's edge, we were now floating in the green waves; the setting sun reflected in the water, moving with the ripples, refracting into countless tiny rays of light, truly a dazzling display of gold and green. We lay back in the rattan chairs, gazing at the surrounding scenery, and our hearts instantly felt relieved, as if we had shed ten thousand bushels of worldly dust.

We chatted casually, and Zhu casually asked me, "How many times have you been here? When was the first time?" I said:

"I can't remember how many times I've been here; but mentioning the first time is quite emotional. It was when I was six or seven years old, living in Yangzhou, and I came with my late father; even though I was a child, I knew how to appreciate the scenery, and I kept asking my father to come, or I would cry; I remember one time, I cried myself to sleep, and when I woke up the next morning, I still clamored for my father, so he哄哄me by saying: He had taken me there last night, but I was sleeping too soundly to wake up; children are children after all, and I actually believed it; but this was also because I had just dreamed of visiting the place." Zhou and Zhu both laughed. But I felt a pang in my heart, and suddenly everything before me became a sad place I couldn't bear to look back on!

The scenery of Little Gold Mountain and Xu Garden remained as before, without any renovation; we each strolled around for a while, and then took a group photo in Xu Garden. It was already dusk, with only a wisp of sunset hanging far on the treetops, and it was clear that night was about to fall. After leaving the garden, we also went to see the newly rebuilt Five Pavilion Bridge, which was indeed ornately carved and brand new; we gazed at it briefly and then set sail back.

Amidst the lights of thousands of homes, we entered the city together and arrived at the Four Five Six Restaurant on Xinsheng Street. There, they have a very famous dish, which is braised carp, especially the braised fish head. We went for dinner just to try this dish. When we ate it, it was indeed well-deserved, just the fish head alone was more than a foot long, covered in fish oil, and cooked to be incredibly tender; eating carp in other places, I had never tasted such a flavor.

Upon parting, Zhu invited me and Zhou: "Let's come to Yangzhou again during the Mid-Autumn Festival, so we can take advantage of the full moon to enjoy a night cruise on the lake; or perhaps next New Year, to explore the plum blossoms at Shi Kefa Shrine." He said, "There are too many places we didn't get to today! Besides the ones we've been to before, there's also the newly built Xiong Garden! By the Mid-Autumn Festival, it should be completed, adding another scenic spot for us to enjoy." At this time, I suddenly remembered the Fifth Spring of Ping Shan Hall, which I had visited several times before, but had completely forgotten to drink the spring water; so I told Zhu, but Zhu said, "The spring water? Don't mention it! The spring has been silted up for almost two years!" This made me feel lost for a long time, and I felt that it had added another regret to my life!
