Shen Bao Medical Journal

Difficulties and Remedies in Rural Health Work

— Ji Bufeng

I've been wandering in Xishan, Jiangxi, and although I've only been serving for a few months, I can't fully understand the situation in rural areas; but I grew up in a rural village in Zhejiang, and after graduating from school, I was also trying to make a living in rural areas. According to what I've personally seen about the current state of rural health, it's probably the same. I dare to talk about my personal shallow views below:

All social construction is based on economics. No matter what item you talk about, you can't do without economics first. Now, rural economic bankruptcy has reached an acute stage. Revitalizing the rural economy is impossible for us little guys working in rural health. There are naturally big people to take on this major responsibility. I can't talk about it, and I won't talk about it; however, in rural health work, we have to consider the current state of the rural economy, choose what is possible for the rural economy, is simple and easy to implement, and is practical, and first guide the farmers to do it, so that everyone can do it and enjoy it, and the results are relatively good. Otherwise, using Westernized ideas to plan various sanitation projects, shutting ourselves up and building carts, is not suitable for use. The results are all impassable, equivalent to a mere formality, only filling the report form nicely, deceiving ourselves.

"It is easier to change mountains and rivers than to alter one's character." These two sentences are not wrong at all. I see that there are many things that farmers can do, but they just don't do them. It's all because it's difficult to change their habits. For example, cleaning the house is quite easy to do, but they just let the dust fill the room and chicken manure cover the ground, and they don't care. They live, eat, and sleep inside and don't feel any discomfort at all. Forming this bad habit was caused by the old society for thousands of years. Improving this bad habit cannot be accomplished in a day or two. We can only adopt a gradual approach, taking the opportunity to promote it. Never be too hasty, otherwise, it will damage the relationship with the farmers: The best way to develop good hygiene habits is to start with children. Now, each Bao school wants to implement a compulsory school system. Each Bao school's children are the entire number of rural children. We should organize a Rural Health Education Committee to promote rural school health so that all children can develop hygiene habits. Schools are group institutions, and it is much more convenient for us to guide them. We can also teach them to do various health promotions, and we can get great help in health education.

Farmers lack scientific knowledge and have little faith in hygiene. Even if we explain the benefits of hygiene in great detail, and say it eloquently, they always listen carefully but disregard it. It is impossible to make a stubborn stone nod. How can we make farmers have faith in hygiene? According to my experience, the best way is to start with treatment. The important mission of rural health work should be to prevent disease, not to treat it, but the main opinion of the farmers is the opposite. They value treatment and despise hygiene. For example, someone in Bao 107 was shot twice, and a woman in Bao 80 committed suicide with scissors, stabbing her throat to a depth of about an inch. After I healed them, they believed that the new medicine was better. After that, it was much smoother for me to work in these two Baos than in other Baos.

Farmers deeply believe in superstition, and all disasters are left to fate. To plant smallpox vaccines, they set up altars to worship the Goddess of Smallpox. When they get sick, they pray in front of the gods for healing. They don't understand the cause of the disease at all. If there is an infectious disease, it is even more pitiful and ridiculous. Those who are sick don't know what infection is and spread it at will, and those who are not sick don't know what infection is and contact it at will, which is bound to spread it greatly. When people are dying everywhere and coffins are in short supply, they can only ask monks and Taoists to draw talismans and perform rituals. It is really a major obstacle to health work. To break superstition and promote hygiene, we must tell the patients face to face when we visit them every day how the disease occurred, what dangers there are, what is the reasonable treatment, and how to prevent it from happening. In addition, we must have the determination to work hard and without complaint, regardless of whether the farmers blame us for offending the gods or scold us to our faces, we must do our best to break superstition, and sometimes we must use political power to prohibit it.

Farmers are ignorant and always regard us as people of another class. Either they underestimate themselves too much and dare not meet us, or they have a suspicious and fearful mentality, fearing that we want to think about money, collect taxes, and send donations, and avoid meeting us. When I first went to each Bao to visit and talk to them, some answered "Yes, yes." to deal with us with perfunctory means, some immediately avoided us, and even when asked where the Bao chief lived, they pretended not to know and refused to tell the truth. Later, after many visits, I gradually became familiar with them and realized that I had no improper demands on them, and then I had the opportunity to talk to them. Because we have a low level of knowledge among the farmers, creating a superior position, promoting work, using this superior position, or political power, and forcing them to do it, may be feasible for a while, but the effect will be lost as soon as the pressure is gone. Not only is it a temporary昙花-like achievement, but it often creates an obstacle to the relationship with the farmers and adds a difficulty to the work. We want to know how health work can penetrate into rural areas, how it can exist permanently, and when we are working in rural health, our attitude should be gentle, our words should be sincere, and it is a way to remedy difficulties in our work.

I recently attended the Rural Health Instructor Conference and listened to reports from various places, and many of the difficulties in the work came from the same workers. We are all the frontline workers in the right rural areas, and such things have happened, which is shameful and disgraceful. Although the organization in each place is divided into health groups, agricultural groups, household affairs groups, cooperative groups, and education groups, each is separated, but in fact, it is the entire rural undertaking. We should broaden our horizons, put the undertaking first, cooperate with each other, and use the spirit of mutual assistance to make the groups work together. The various difficulties mentioned above can be easily broken, and the work can be advanced. It is not only the luck of health work, but also the benefit of each group.

Causes and Treatment of Insomnia

— Translated by Zifu

In order to maintain their lives and engage in activity, humans must have a certain amount of time for wakefulness and sleep to alternate with each other. That is to say, after a certain period of activity, activity must be stopped in order to eliminate fatigue and restore physical strength. That is sleep. If sleep is uncomfortable or impaired, then a person's ability to live will be greatly reduced. If sleep is hindered to the extreme, it will be difficult to even maintain life. Therefore, a healthy person has a very regular alternation of day and night, that is to say, a very regular alternation of sleep and wakefulness, in order to smoothly maintain his life and activity.

So, how much sleep does a so-called healthy person need every day? It can be said that this varies from person to person. Generally speaking, young children need a longer period of sleep, and then as they grow up, the amount of sleep gradually decreases.

Generally speaking, young children need from ten to twelve hours of sleep each day; adults need from seven to eight hours; and the elderly need less time.

If we carefully observe the sleep state of a healthy person, we can discover that the depth of sleep undergoes various forms of change over different periods of time. The deepest sleep is one to two hours after falling asleep, after which it gradually becomes shallower, and then near dawn, it enters a slightly deeper sleep state again. This is one type. Another type is that the deepest sleep is two to three hours after falling asleep, and after continuing for a short time, it gradually becomes shallower, and near dawn, one wakes up.

As mentioned above, in a healthy state, the onset of sleep is at a certain time. From this, one can rest and recover from fatigue in order to continue future activities. However, if sleep is impaired in a certain disease state, then insomnia occurs.

In insomnia, one type is that it is difficult to fall asleep after lying in bed; another type is that the state of falling asleep is relatively good, but one feels very tired when waking up in the morning; and another type is that one sleeps very lightly at night and wakes up frequently. In addition, there is a mixed type in which it is not easy to fall asleep, and sleep is very light and easy to wake up, and one is extremely tired when getting up in the morning. Before discussing how to deal with insomnia, we must carefully observe the type of insomnia.

There are various causes of insomnia. For example, diseases of the brain, mental illness, poisoning from various drugs or toxins, the pain or pain of other diseases in the body, severe coughing and wheezing, gastrointestinal disorders, urinary disorders!……etc., all have the potential to cause insomnia. However, strictly speaking, so-called insomnia should be a condition in which insomnia is the main and only symptom. This symptom is often influenced by mental excitement. Especially in young and middle-aged people, this is the most common cause of insomnia. Also, it is caused by mental fatigue, such as insomnia in neurotic people. However, one thing should be noted here is that often some causes are the same, but the reactions they cause in each person are very different. For example, some minor events are not enough to cause insomnia in some people; but in others, they can cause extreme mental excitement, resulting in insomnia. Since the reactions caused by events are so different for each person, the causes of insomnia are naturally not easy to define in general. We can only carefully examine each person to find out the cause and seek a way to deal with it.

The causes of mental excitement include mental fatigue, depression, worry, self-blame, disappointment, fear, grief… etc. The most important of these are fear, depression, and worry. For example, students prepare desperately for exams and study until late at night. As a result, when they go to bed, they still have residual mental excitement, which can greatly interfere with falling asleep.

However, if one studies without reaching the point of mental fatigue, of course, the above situation will not occur. However, if various worries and fears are added to it, it can also become an important cause of insomnia.

The first step in dealing with insomnia is to remove the causes of mental excitement as much as possible. Try to resolve family disputes, job dissatisfaction, and business failures that can lead to fear, depression, anxiety, self-blame, grief, and disappointment. It is true that it is not easy to solve such great difficulties by relying on the parties alone. Therefore, the help of everyone around is indispensable.

Generally speaking, most people with insomnia are neurotic. For these people, even minor events can become a cause of insomnia, so it is best to avoid stimulants as much as possible. At the same time, the temperature of the bedroom should be appropriate, the air circulation should be good, sounds and money should be avoided as much as possible, dinner should not be too full, and tea, coffee, and wine should not be drunk at night. Regular urination and defecation and a fixed bedtime are all very important. All of this should be given deep attention. In addition, we must try our best to avoid mental fatigue at night. Especially for students, even when they are very busy, they should avoid overworking themselves. They must stop for a certain amount of time and rest a little before going to bed.

Sometimes, when the neurasthenia or fatigue reaches a deeper level, it is best to leave the job temporarily and go to a quieter place to recuperate. However, in this case, the coast and high mountains are not suitable. Because there are many things that can cause insomnia in those places. However, if there is no way to change the location to recuperate and leave the job, then one has to set a certain amount of rest time during the day or engage in drawing. It is also very beneficial to do outdoor gymnastics during the day.

Any continuous, mild, and monotonous stimulus, such as listening to monotonous and gentle music, counting numbers, counting breaths, etc., can help sleep. Similarly, mild electrical friction or artificial friction on the whole body can also help sleep.

Bathing in lukewarm water for a long time is also effective for helping sleep. If electrical friction or artificial massage can be continued after bathing, it is even better. Also, after soaking in warm water, wrap the whole body in a dry towel, and then wrap a towel around it, and rest for about thirty minutes to calm the mind, which is also very conducive to sleep.

Page 18

Finally, let's talk about sleeping pills. If it is possible not to use them, it is best not to use them, and to try to help sleep with other methods. If it is absolutely necessary to use them, then if they are slightly effective after taking them, they can be discarded immediately and other methods can be used. Also, when taking sleeping pills, you should use drugs with the least side effects. It is best to take a small amount. Moreover, the types of drugs should be changed frequently. It is not very wise for people to purchase certain drugs on hand and take them at will. Because doing so, on the one hand, one is accustomed to using one drug, so one needs to gradually increase the dosage, eventually leading to poisoning; on the other hand, one is accustomed to relying on drugs, and in the future, one may not be able to sleep without drugs. Therefore, one must first be guided by a doctor before taking them.

Among sleeping pills, one type takes effect quickly and the drug's power disappears early; another type takes effect late and the drug's power lasts longer. For people who have difficulty falling asleep, it is advisable to use the former; for people who sleep lightly and are easy to wake up early, it is better to use the latter. For mixed-type insomnia, it is reasonable to use these two drugs in combination. However, this must be handled by a doctor, and it is easiest to make a big mistake if ordinary people mix them at will.

Also, sleeping pills must be taken according to the time and method specified by the doctor. Impatient people take it immediately when they cannot fall asleep at night. This not only has no effect, but also often brings various uncomfortable side effects the next morning.

In short, it is the most foolish method to only abuse drugs to seek sleep without removing the causative factors.

Common Sense Q&A About Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(Eighty-six) Liver Abscess

What is a liver abscess?

Liver abscess is a disease in which the liver becomes purulent, so it is also called Suppurative Hepatitis.

What causes liver abscesses?

Most of them are secondary to purulent diseases in other parts of the body, such as intestinal ulcers, amoebic dysentery, appendicitis, septic pericarditis, pulmonary gangrene, putrid bronchitis, purulent cholecystitis, gallstones, ascariasis, etc. Some are also caused by trauma.

When a liver abscess is very small in the affected area, what symptoms does the patient have?

If the abscess is very small, even if it is multiple, it does not cause any symptoms.

When the liver abscess becomes larger, what does the patient feel?

The patient complains of a dull or severe pain in the liver area, radiating to the right shoulder.

What symptoms does he have?

The symptoms he feels are an enlarged liver, an elevated diaphragm, reduced respiratory movement at the lung boundary, difficulty breathing, vomiting, and hiccups. If the liver enlarges downwards, the rib arch bulges, sometimes presenting with fluctuations, with hypersensitivity or severe pain. Touching it causes coughing.

Does the patient have a fever?

In most cases, there is a chill followed by a fever. But some do not have a fever.

Does the patient with a liver abscess also have an enlarged spleen?

The spleen is usually not enlarged.

Does jaundice occur?

Most of them do not occur either; but sometimes jaundice can occur because the bile duct is compressed.

Are there any abnormalities in the patient's blood?

When there is a liver abscess, the number of white blood cells in the blood increases.

What is the course of this disease?

It varies depending on the original disease. If the original disease is septic, it is mostly acute and takes an unfortunate turn. If the original disease is gallstones, then it takes a chronic course. It also often ruptures into the intestinal tract, trachea, or abdominal wall.

How is a liver abscess diagnosed?

If it is suspected, a test puncture must be performed to see if pus is drawn out. Because it is often difficult to distinguish from infectious cholangitis, gallbladder empyema, and abscesses near the liver.

What is the prognosis of this disease?

Most are bad and often fatal.

What is the treatment?

In addition to the fact that emetine injection must be performed for amoebic dysentery, other cases generally require surgical operation, incision and drainage, but the results cannot be expected to be very hopeful.

Common Sense of Ear, Nose, Throat and Eye Diseases

— Tang Renzhen

(Ninety-one) Pupillary Reaction

The pupillary reaction is originally a special function possessed by the iris. It is caused by the interaction of the pupillary sphincter muscle and the pupillary dilator muscle. Its reaction is a reflex. Therefore, the pupillary reaction cannot be regulated by our will. The pupillary reaction is of great significance in the diagnosis of internal medicine diseases. It often provides valuable assistance to doctors. The pupillary reaction can be divided into two types: pupillary constriction reaction and pupillary dilation reaction. Among them, the pupillary constriction reaction can be further divided into light reaction, convergence reaction, palpebral fissure closure reaction, and trigeminal nerve reflex. They are specially described as follows.

Light Reaction When we shine light on the pupil in a dark room, it can immediately cause pupillary constriction. This is the so-called light reaction. This pupillary constriction movement is caused by the connection of the optic nerve and the oculomotor nerve nucleus. There are two other types of light reactions. One is the reaction caused by light entering the pupil, called the direct reaction. The reaction caused by the other eye is called the indirect reaction. The two reactions often occur simultaneously. The duration of the reaction is half to one second.

Convergence Reaction The subject is asked to look into the distance first. Suddenly, he is asked to look at a point at a considerable distance in front of him again. Then the pupil will constrict immediately. This is the so-called convergence reaction. This pupillary constriction movement is a common movement in the area controlled by the oculomotor nerve.

Palpebral Fissure Closure Reaction When the palpebral fissure is strongly closed. Constriction of the pupil often occurs. This is caused by the common movement of the orbicularis oculi muscle of the eyelid.

Trigeminal Nerve Reflex When the trigeminal nerve area of the conjunctiva, cornea, and iris is stimulated. Pupillary constriction often occurs. Therefore, pupillary constriction can often be observed in cases of conjunctivitis, keratitis, corneal foreign bodies, and iritis.

In addition, the pupil often constricts during sleep or anesthesia. This is called sleep constriction.

Pupillary Dilation Reaction When mental excitement occurs or another part of the body receives a sensation (such as surprise or pain). Pupillary dilation can often occur through reflex action.

Tooth Knowledge Q&A (34)

— Lin Jianxian

Chapter 7 Treatment of Dental Diseases

(Question 171) Can the people in our country who traditionally "catch tooth worms" really treat tooth decay and toothache?

Answer: As mentioned in Question 63, the cause of tooth decay is not a visible "tooth worm." Because our people have traditionally lacked knowledge of bacteriology, they saw that the decay of fruits, wood, bamboo, etc., is sometimes caused by worms, and therefore assumed that teeth were the same. Unscrupulous people take advantage of this absurd psychology and create many fraudulent methods, claiming to be able to catch tooth worms and treat tooth decay and toothache. Even today, those who make a living from this are still all over the country. This is truly a strange phenomenon in the civilized world! If they can really catch living tooth worms, these worms are definitely not originally in the patient's mouth; they brought them themselves. They are completely deceiving ignorant people.

(Question 172) Some people say that after treatment by "catching tooth worms," the pain of tooth decay is immediately reduced. What is the reason for this?

Answer: Those who "catch tooth worms" often use a copper needle to pierce the gums, releasing a lot of blood, claiming it is "poisonous blood." In this way, the congestion of the affected tooth is reduced, and the pain will naturally be slightly alleviated. However, this is a temporary phenomenon, and the disease is not cured. Soon, the pain will return as before. Moreover, piercing the gums with a non-disinfected copper needle is very dangerous.

Section 3 Treatment of Periodontitis

(Question 173) How should non-infectious periodontitis be treated?

Answer: If it is caused by local irritants, the irritants should be removed first. If it is caused by arthritis, syphilis, or internal medicine, systemic treatment must be used. Methods to alleviate pain that patients can do themselves include: applying iodine or aconite tincture to the outside of the gums near the affected tooth; taking painkillers internally; soaking feet in hot water for half an hour each time.

(Question 174) How should acute infectious periodontitis (i.e., alveolar abscess) be treated?

Answer: In the early stage, the treatment should involve opening the pulp chamber, connecting the root canal, rinsing with disinfectant, and sealing with disinfectant. Apply aconite tincture and iodine to the outside of the gums. At the same time, use laxatives, sudorifics, and hot foot soaks. The purpose of all these methods is to reduce inflammation and relieve pain. However, if pus accumulates and cannot be eliminated, methods should be used to promote its early maturation and then incision and drainage should be performed, and all symptoms will disappear. During the process, if the pain is severe or insomnia occurs, painkillers and sleeping pills should be taken. Laxatives should be used to keep bowel movements regular. And the mouth should be kept as clean as possible, and mouthwash should be used frequently.

Although there are various rules and regulations in place, due to a lack of knowledge or understanding of the purpose of the laws, the effectiveness is limited. Each office will teach simple disinfection methods, communicable diseases, public health, and regulations for each industry, as well as methods for implementing the New Life Movement in each industry.

Cleanliness is the preliminary and basic condition for health. In addition, public places will be inspected on the 27th and 28th, also jointly carried out by the above-mentioned agencies.

The Preparatory Committee will focus on the above-mentioned tasks. Since the launch of preparations, a total of three plenary meetings and one meeting for each committee have been held. All the facilities for the general assembly are roughly planned. The chairman and the secretary-general and deputy secretary-general are responsible for carrying out the work. The activities of this session of the assembly are expected to be outlined as follows:

Performance Aspect: With children's health and maternal and infant health as the center, central activities will be scheduled at the venue every day, and relevant agencies and groups will be invited to participate in performances, and recreational activities or movies will be used to add to the fun.

Promotion Aspect: The promotion work occupies an important position in this health campaign, and the organization is more complicated. The contents include cleanliness campaigns, labor services, health knowledge training for general public places, inspection of public places, and a campaign to discourage spitting, and promotion of factory hygiene.

In short: This health campaign takes into account the needs of the times. Its work should be multi-faceted rather than local; it should have a central activity, but not be biased. Based on this policy, it should be able to avoid mistakes. As the opening approaches, we still invite all sectors of society to teach us. I am most fortunate.

The Meaning and Several Important Methods of Factory Hygiene

— Li Xuanguo

The Shanghai 15th Health Campaign has designated today as Factory Hygiene Publicity Day, and I have been asked to give a speech on publicity. You are all leaders in the industrial and labor sectors of this city, and I believe you will pay significant attention to this issue. Let's first explain the meaning of the term "factory hygiene." We all know that the term "factory hygiene" is already just a habitually used term and cannot encompass the entire scope of work. Taking the layout plan of this exhibition as an example, we want to present the contributions of the city's health administration to our life process in order. Therefore, our overall title is "Health and Life." The first part is "Infant Hygiene," building a good foundation for health from pregnancy and birth. As age increases, when the time comes for schooling, "School Hygiene" begins, which is the second part. After completing studies, it is time for a career; in a narrow sense, not everyone goes to work in a factory after graduation. The term "factory hygiene" does not seem to represent all hygiene work during the career period. However, in a broad sense, while one works in a factory, it cannot be said that those not in a factory are not working; work is always the same. Some people want to divide brain work and physical work into two types, which is a mistake. We all know now that physical labor, especially with the application of modern machinery, cannot do without brain work. Brain work sometimes requires considerable physical strength to cope. Also, there is a very accurate proof that there is not much difference between brain work and physical work: regardless of brain work or physical work, when exceeding the capacity range, there is a feeling of fatigue, which is a physiological problem that we do not need to discuss in depth for now. Therefore, it seems more appropriate to replace "factory hygiene" with "occupational hygiene." As mentioned above, we will temporarily follow the customary application and discuss the historical evolution of factory hygiene.

Historical Progress of Factory Hygiene: Our country is based on agriculture. The development of factories has only been a recent phenomenon in the past ten years or so. If we examine the situation in advanced European and American countries that are dominant in industry, there has only been a systematic history of more than a century. In 1767 AD, about 170 years ago, due to the invention of the spinning machine, there was already a large-scale textile industry. At that time, it was still the era of slavery. Workers worked 16 hours a day, were whipped and chained, and were secretly buried upon death. Society regarded factories as places of all evil. A British statistic shows that in 1833 AD, in Manchester, a major industrial town, the average lifespan of workers was only 22 years. In better societies in the town, the average lifespan was 44 years, a difference of more than double. Furthermore, the national mortality rate in Britain at that time was 22 per thousand, while in industrial areas, it was 36 per thousand. At that time, some people regarded factories as slaughterhouses, which cannot be said to be an exaggeration. Relief plans therefore gradually developed. In 1802 AD, Britain passed a factory law in Parliament. The main points of the law are briefly listed as follows: workers should not work more than 12 hours a day; workers should be issued two sets of clothes per year; workers must have the opportunity to study; apprentices must be registered; factory buildings must be whitewashed twice a year; and regular inspections must be conducted by judges or priests. Later, there was gradual progress. Importantly, in 1833 AD, the British government appointed factory inspectors. In 1844, the age of child labor and the employment of female workers were restricted. In 1847, female workers and child laborers could not work more than 10 hours a day. In 1854, the Factory Safety Law was promulgated. Later, there were restrictions on dangerous occupations and the employment of female and child laborers, and then gradually became more complete. The above is the situation in Britain. Other European countries have also made equal efforts. For example, the Berlin Museum of Industrial Hygiene in Germany (established in 1904) and the Vienna Museum of Industrial Hygiene (established in 1909) show in detail the relationship between industry and health, diseases and dangers, their causes, and prevention methods, which is worth commemorating. The completion of social insurance in 1913 was also an important milestone in factory hygiene. The starting point of industrial hygiene in the United States was the protection of child labor. In 1888, there were factory inspection commissioners. The government established many associations to study the hygiene and safety issues of industry, and the results were very excellent. What is noteworthy in the past twenty years is that various factories have voluntarily participated in or sought to improve various industrial hygiene issues. The attitude of refusing factory inspections in the past has completely changed. It is generally recognized that factory hygiene benefits both labor and capital. The above facts tell us that the history of factory hygiene can be divided into three periods: The first period is the dark age, where capitalists only seek to increase production to make huge profits; workers are completely in a state of oppression. The second period is the relief period, where many philanthropists, based on compassion, try to relieve generally devastated members of society. They strive to enact laws, and the implementation of laws mostly sympathizes with the workers and takes a more restrictive attitude towards capitalists. Recently, it has entered the third period, which can be said to be the economization period of factory hygiene. Everyone unanimously agrees that attention to factory hygiene not only directly benefits labor but also indirectly benefits capital economically. Lips and teeth support each other and are mutually beneficial. We consider this type of progress to be very satisfactory, because no matter what business, economic benefits are always happily accepted. Therefore, we can be very optimistic about the future of factory hygiene. (To be continued in tomorrow's Xinwen Bao)

Supplement to the Shanghai edition of Shen Bao

Talk

Recalling the Scientific Examinations of the Imperial Era

— Jing

I have never been interested in sports. I never care about news about the sports world, such as someone breaking a record or someone breaking another record. So, I don't know anything about sports, let alone have the qualifications to criticize or comment.

However, the recent selection of athletes has made it impossible for me not to say a few words. The selection of athletes for the World Games has been criticized thoroughly in the newspapers since the selection committee announced the results. Some say "the election is unfair," others say "the election is fraudulent," some say "the selection is questionable," and others say "it is self-deception." It is truly chaotic and confusing, and I am deeply puzzled.

The selection of athletes should have certain standards. How high they jump, how far they run, how much time they spend, those who pass are naturally selected, and those who fail are naturally eliminated. Even if many fail, then those who jump the highest, run the farthest, and spend the least time among those who fail are selected. This is an ironclad law. With thousands of people pointing fingers and all eyes watching, no matter how bold and powerful the selection committee is, they should not dare to reverse right and wrong and select arbitrarily.

At first, I was a little suspicious, suspecting that the unsuccessful candidates were jealous or that they were being nitpicky due to regional relations, which is also a possible situation. Later, after examining the facts, I found that I was completely wrong. It was entirely the selection committee abusing their power and acting emotionally that led to the unanimous attack from the sports world. The selection committee also knew that they were in the wrong and had no excuse, and that the selection was erroneous. However, they still refused to correct their mistakes. The public criticism from the media clearly shows that there was no personal interest involved. However, the selection of athletes for the World Games is extremely important. Internally, it encourages the martial spirit of the people of the whole country; externally, it wipes away the shame of being the "sick man of East Asia." Now, the selection committee disregards public opinion and insists on going its own way, which is extremely disappointing.

First, the reason why our country must organize a selection committee to select athletes to participate in the World Games is to obtain a fair and accurate selection of talents. Recently, European countries have been working exceptionally hard on sports, so their level is very high. If our athletes want to participate in the World Games, even if we select top-notch talents, it is still difficult to compete with strong enemies. Now, they abandon the superior and choose the inferior. I don't know what the selection committee is thinking.

Second, there are dozens of countries participating in this World Games. The winning of championships is closely related to national prestige. Therefore, recently, when the African-American boxer Joe Louis was defeated by the German Schmeling, the German Propaganda Minister Goebbels immediately sent a telegram to congratulate him, saying, "Your victory is Germany's victory. It is an honor for you to win glory for the leader Hitler." Conversely, your failure is Germany's failure. Now, our country's selection of athletes abandons the superior and takes the mediocre. Is the selection committee's intention to win glory for the country? Or is it willing for the country to fail?

Third, this time our country is participating in the World Games in Germany, and I heard that the total expenses will be as high as two or three hundred thousand yuan. In this time of poverty and financial exhaustion, raising this money is not easy. Now, the selection committee is acting entirely on emotion and does not choose fairly. The results of this competition are self-evident. Therefore, using hundreds of thousands of yuan to cater to the feelings of a few people is not only a waste of money, but also makes the selection a superfluous act. It would be better to choose a few people from the relatives and friends of the selection committee. Why bother with the formality of selection?

Therefore, I am reminded of the imperial examinations of the Qing Dynasty. Everyone knows the evils of the imperial examinations, such as cheating, impersonation, and bribery. They are so appalling that they are condemned. The imperial examinations were therefore abolished. But if the chief examiner was impeached by the censor and found guilty, he would be dismissed from office at best and beheaded at worst. The grand ceremony of selecting talents was not a trivial matter. The difference between the current selection of athletes for the World Games is only a few points. In the past, officials found guilty of corruption would be punished, but now members of the selection committee can be corrupt without being held responsible. In the past, corruption was a secret act, but now corruption can be blatant. When the country has reached this point, those with power wield it without any scruples. Therefore, the imperial examination system can be abolished, but it should not be abolished.

Loquat

— Ji Nan

In front of my study is a courtyard surrounded by walls on three sides, less than a zhang wide. Looking out from the window of the study, the sky is only a narrow square, truly worthy of being called a "well-bottom view." However, a loquat tree miraculously grows in this well.

Loquat, the loquat that comes with the depressing plum rains. It does not have the sour taste of plums, and it is the most popular fruit in early summer.

How could this lovely fruit tree grow in this narrow courtyard? It is not only mismatched, but also

Page 22

Simply too "humiliating," so it must be said to be an "anomaly."

So, what is the story behind this "anomaly"? The story is like this.

I don't know what year it was, and I don't know who it was, but someone casually threw a loquat pit that had just been spat out of their mouth into this courtyard. Later, this tree grew. At first, when it was just a small tree that had just grown, no one could say that its predecessor was a loquat pit, and no one could recognize what kind of tree it was. Some said it was a peach tree, others said it was a plum tree, a pear tree..., it was not until it bore its first fruit that it explained itself.

"The unintentionally planted willow will flourish," it turned out that this was a genuine loquat tree!

Due to the limitations of the three surrounding walls, the tree lost the freedom to grow. Its trunk is very tall, and its branches and leaves only open up above the height of the wall, forming a long-handled canopy, unlike what is seen in ordinary orchards.

Therefore, when the fruits are ripe, although the clusters of golden yellow orbs in the reflection of the green leaves begin to entice me, they are "out of reach." I can only watch the birds peck at them and "see but not touch."

Therefore, these lovely golden yellow loquats, in my eyes, are just beautiful flowers in full bloom. I can only feast my eyes on them but not my stomach. When they are ripe and fall off automatically, are they not like withered and fallen petals? However, when I see it shining brightly in the sunlight, I cannot help but "salivate" and "sigh under the tree."

"Salivating" is a sign of not being thirsty. I did not expect that loquats, like plums, have the unexpected effect of quenching thirst.

Ah Gen (Continued)

— Zhuo Er

If one were to admit that she was a "five dollar foreign girl," then when she drew the pale green curtains at night, someone should commend her "business" as being good. Every few days there was such an occasion, at which time she was like a skillful magician, conjuring up a person with whom she only had a "five dollar foreign" relationship. She giggled, allowing him to tease and fondle her... and then she would draw the curtains. What a discordant picture this was! Painted on the canvas of "five dollar foreign" ugliness.

Recently, Ah Gen has rarely been seen walking in the alley during the day, so the men felt a bit of loneliness and boredom, while the women were happy. They cursed this charming vixen, wishing she would hurry up and die, so that they could be relieved of the responsibility of guarding their beloved men. But, contrary to their expectations, Ah Gen would still gracefully pass through the alley, and what made them even more jealous was that she dressed even more beautifully. Busy-bodies finally found out that she was now having a passionate affair with the boss of a certain store.

Many days later, on a clear morning, the alley was filled with people, mischievous children, idle men and women, clamoring as if something major had happened. A chubby middle-aged woman, gesticulating, cursed: "Shameless, seducing other people's men... rotten cunt." She was pointing at Ah Gen's room, which made it clear that the chubby woman must be the boss's wife! At the same time, many other women were helping her by shouting curses like: "Rotten cunt who steals other people's husbands..." and other embarrassing words. People were laughing and jeering. Even young girls, with red faces, squeezed into the crowd to inquire about what was going on... Everyone was surrounded by a wave of playful mockery.

"Get out here! Rotten cunt, I'll beat you to death..." the chubby boss's wife yelled, her face red and her neck thick. "Get out here!..."

Suddenly, unexpectedly, Ah Gen rushed out with her hair disheveled. Tears streamed down her face, followed by her elderly mother. She stood with imposing air, hands on her hips, pointing a finger at the chubby woman:

"Who are you cursing? Huh, what rotten this and rotten that! I'm not seducing your man, to tell you the truth, I... I want his money... We're poor... I have an old mother, an old father at home... and a little brother! ...They all need money! ...Who hasn't seen your stinky man? No one wants to seduce him, he comes willingly himself, and I take the money! ...Hmph, that's nothing to be ashamed of, don't you all have men too? ...You're the shameless ones! ...Rotten! Aren't you rotten? Aren't you rotten?..."

Before she could finish speaking, the chubby woman, mumbling something, waved her hand, and then she, and the women who had come with her, rushed forward and dragged Ah Gen to the ground. ... (To be continued next Saturday)

Yellow Skin

— Chou Tong

The orange-yellow sun shone slantingly on Black Bone Two's thatched hut. From the woods, occasional breezes blew, very cool, without a hint of summer heat.

Black Bone Two took his big-headed bamboo pipe, sat down on a green stone slab in front of the door, sighed painfully, then opened his water pipe box, pinched out a thumb-sized ball of tobacco, pressed it onto the pipe, lit it, and sucked hard. Light smoke was exhaled from his withered mouth as he breathed, like several small green dragons swimming, but it immediately disintegrated and disappeared. ...

"Doo! Doo yo!"

Suddenly, a burst of rapid yelling broke the surrounding silence. A long-distance bus rushed past. Along with the smoke behind the bus came a gust of "Kreosote" stink.

"Damn his mother, stinky fart bug!"

Black Bone Two cursed angrily. The four heavy rubber wheels of the bus passing by him seemed to be grinding his heart. He wished he could knock it over with his pipe.

Two years ago, Black Bone Two was still well-off. He had a two-section single-entrance tile-roofed house and a yellow-skin orchard.

One day, he was returning from the street carrying an empty cargo basket. His son, his eyes pregnant with a terrifying light of melancholy, approached him and said:

Broadcast Script

Suzhou People (24)

— Written by Gu Wenzong

Jinghong: Why shouldn't it be added? Is there something to be avoided?

Liya: That's natural, what I hate is Suzhou, don't you know?

Jinghong: I know you hate Suzhou, but I don't know why you started calling me Suzhou Sister?

Liya: The reason I call you Suzhou Sister is because of what that Suzhou Sister said on the ship: it's completely flattery! Good at flattering and complimenting people; that's a unique trait of Suzhou people! Suzhou Sister, don't you think so?

Liya: You don't need to ask me, since you already understand, why do I need to explain it to you again? I won't talk to you anymore, goodbye.

Jinghong: This is the third "goodbye," do you want another "goodbye"? (Said and laughed for a while)

Liya: I absolutely can't let you make fun of me, I'm leaving, no need to see me off! No need! (The sound of leather shoes moving away).

Note:

All sounds in the car gradually fade away, until there is no sound at all.
